    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

  <span id="freeText7456734042204894503" style="display:none"><i>This is an alternate cover edition for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25674863-tattered-on-my-sleeve" rel="nofollow noopener">B00YZ8M3A8</a> </i><br /><br /><b>I had her first.<br />I fell in love with her.<br />Then we fucked everything up.</b><br /><br />Warning: This is not a "typical" romance. It's not even a typical MC Romance.<br /><br /><i>Lust.</i><br />Eight years ago, the Lost Kings, MC was recovering from turmoil within the club Wrath and Trinity met. Their connection was instant and explosive.<br /><br /><i>Fury.</i><br />Wrath and Trinity's story is a heart-breaking, soul-crushing, tear-your-heart-into-pieces story. The way they hurt each other over the years is intense, raw, frustrating and sometimes dark.<p><br /><i>Forgiveness.</i><br />Can they move past their horrible pasts to become better people and ultimately forgive each other?</p><p><br /><br />They’ve wasted too many years. Once Wrath learns the dark secret that’s been fueling Trinity for years, he’ll stop at nothing to prove they’re meant to be together and that she’s worthy of the love she keeps denying.<br /></p><p><br />Tattered on My Sleeve is a full-length novel at over 145,000 word<br />(567 pages). It is book #4 in the popular Lost Kings MC series, but it can be read first or as a stand-alone.</p></span>

    <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake"><img alt="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605987751p2/11626803.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1316384825?book_show_action=true">Jun 24, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake">Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780990794561" href="/book/show/23662114-tattered-on-my-sleeve">review of another edition</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1316384825" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18292901292174233593"><b>Re-read: 12/16/19...</b><br/><br/><u>Original Review:</u><br/><br/><b>4 Stars</b><br/><br/>This is a little different than some of the usual MC Club..."fare" in that the heroine, Trinity, is not a lawyer...<br/><br/>...a biker's daughter...<br/><br/>...or anything like that...<br/><br/>She's a Club Girl. <br/><br/>And we all know what <i>that</i> means.<br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438709202i/15745558.jpg' width='400' height='506' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Home girl gets around a little bit.</b> <br/><br/>Now pipe down all you "don't slut-shame" psychopaths.<br/> <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428071818i/14358657.jpg' width='430' height='299' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>I'm not slut-shaming, people.</b><br/><br/>Cause you know, sexual revolution, women's rights, yadda, yadda yadda.<br/><br/>My point here - there really is one, I swear - is </span>
  <span id="freeText18292901292174233593" style="display:none"><b>Re-read: 12/16/19...</b><br><br><u>Original Review:</u><br><br><b>4 Stars</b><br><br>This is a little different than some of the usual MC Club..."fare" in that the heroine, Trinity, is not a lawyer...<br><br>...a biker's daughter...<br><br>...or anything like that...<br><br>She's a Club Girl. <br><br>And we all know what <i>that</i> means.<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438709202i/15745558.jpg" width="400" height="506" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Home girl gets around a little bit.</b> <br><br>Now pipe down all you "don't slut-shame" psychopaths.<br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428071818i/14358657.jpg" width="430" height="299" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I'm not slut-shaming, people.</b><br><br>Cause you know, sexual revolution, women's rights, yadda, yadda yadda.<br><br>My point here - there really is one, I swear - is that Trinity and Wrath's story is a little different than the norm in that they fuck other people during the course of their own love story. <br><br>NOT my favorite scenario. <br><br>But, having read book one, I already knew that would be the case and still wanted to read Trinity and Wrath's book. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442949165i/16297273._SX540_.jpg" width="480" height="428.8" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And I could attempt to make it through this book.<br><br>#TeamBritBrit<br><br>And I'm glad I did.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442949744i/16297349._SX540_.jpg" width="468.75" height="403.5" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Even though I sometimes got really fucking annoyed with the actions of these two ass-hats and how they allowed their relationship to get to the point it did...<br><br>...especially Trinity... <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1441823449ra/16156691.gif" width="320" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>...we eventually discover more about Trinity and her past. <br><br>And why she is the way she is. <br><br>And in the end, it was really cool to watch her and Wrath come together and see to how much he cared about her. <br><br>Their connection was truly palpable for me and I really enjoyed it. <br><br>I'm looking forward to the next book in the series...<br><br>...and I feel compelled to go back now and read books two and three - which I originally skipped because they are about the same couple as book one - however, there were shenanigans between <i>those</i> two in this book that apparently occurred in those previous books (as parts of this book overlapped with all three of those previous books) and I find myself curious...<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1440778533ra/16023356.gif" width="500" height="281" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1390158664" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8427145490483300427">BLOODY HELL. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1460493219ra/18749183.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>This is what I call a true MC romance. Angst. Heartbreak. Hate. Love. Drama. Dysfunction. Bleeding-out-on-the-floor painful.<br/><br/>The first part of the book can be described with one word: chaos. It almost ruined me. I’m an angst addict, I thrive on it. But that was almost too much even for me. God, what Wrath and Trinity did to each other. It was pure torture. It hurt like hell reading about it but in some sick and twisted way I loved every second of it.<br/><br/>If you survive the first part, th</span>
  <span id="freeText8427145490483300427" style="display:none">BLOODY HELL. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1460493219ra/18749183.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>This is what I call a true MC romance. Angst. Heartbreak. Hate. Love. Drama. Dysfunction. Bleeding-out-on-the-floor painful.<br><br>The first part of the book can be described with one word: chaos. It almost ruined me. I’m an angst addict, I thrive on it. But that was almost too much even for me. God, what Wrath and Trinity did to each other. It was pure torture. It hurt like hell reading about it but in some sick and twisted way I loved every second of it.<br><br>If you survive the first part, the second part is less dramatic but still painful and gripping. Here the story gets slow. There are a lot of details, every moment is mentioned and every event is thoroughly described. But this is how it is supposed to be. Because the details and internal thoughts help you understand the characters and their story. Because forgiving is a painful and slow process.<br><br>The third and final part focuses on healing and learning to trust each other. It’s where you really fall in love with each of the characters. And although there’s only a happy-for-now ending, you’ll feel satisfied and at peace.<br><br>This book is not for everybody. If you don’t like long and slow books with lots of drama, heartbreak and high angst levels, then this book is not for you.<br><br><b>QUICK REVIEW:</b><br><br><b>Enjoyment:</b> 5/5<br><b>Writing style:</b> 4/5<br><b>Storyline:</b> 4/5 <br><b>Hero:</b> 5/5<br><b>Heroine:</b> 4/5<br><b>Secondary characters:</b> 5/5 <br><b>Hotness/steam:</b> 4/5 <br><b>Romance:</b> 4/5 <br><b>Angst:</b> 5/5<br><b>Darkness level:</b> 3/5<br><b>Humor:</b> 3/5<br><b> Depth of the book:</b> 4/5<br><b>POV:</b> dual, 1st person<br><b> Triggers:</b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[explicit sex scenes with other people <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b> Recommended for:</b> fans of Madeline Sheehan (Undeniable series), Nicole Jacquelyn (The Aces series)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510504825i/24426022._SX540_.jpg" width='400"/' class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1346478629" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1346478629" />
    <a title="Lauren" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9920920-lauren"><img alt="Lauren" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1471373646p2/9920920.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1346478629?book_show_action=true">Jul 26, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lauren" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lauren" href="/user/show/9920920-lauren">Lauren</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780990794561" href="/book/show/23662114-tattered-on-my-sleeve">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1346478629" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14794229464073481162"><a href='http://www.saintsnsinnersbooks.com' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429281707i/14563741._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Autumn… here’s my heart… you ripped it out. <br/><br/>I knew going in that Tattered on My Sleeve would be so far different than Rock and Hope’s. Yes, Rock and Hope’s romance was far from traditional and full of angtsy twists. Yet, Wrath and Trinity’s story both broke and shocked me. These two characters set themselves not only on a collision course from the first time they meet, but on a path of self-destruction. <br/><br/>Trinity may come off as a club girl, but she really isn’t. The club protects her and she </span>
  <span id="freeText14794229464073481162" style="display:none"><a href="http://www.saintsnsinnersbooks.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429281707i/14563741._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Autumn… here’s my heart… you ripped it out. <br><br>I knew going in that Tattered on My Sleeve would be so far different than Rock and Hope’s. Yes, Rock and Hope’s romance was far from traditional and full of angtsy twists. Yet, Wrath and Trinity’s story both broke and shocked me. These two characters set themselves not only on a collision course from the first time they meet, but on a path of self-destruction. <br><br>Trinity may come off as a club girl, but she really isn’t. The club protects her and she in turn, helps run the club house. Her sexual exploits during her self-inflicted destruction phase are hot as hell, but painful to read at the same time. You know where her true feelings lie, but he’s someone that she can’t have. She settles for hook ups as she painfully watches his own exploits. Wrath on the other hand takes one misunderstanding and runs with his misguided notation. His heart aches every single time Trinity goes with another one of his brothers in leather, but she made her choice in his eyes. He’s a tortured soul with a heart of gold, and I loved him for it. <br><br>Autumn has taken her unique MC premise and added so much to the story. Wrath and Trinity’s romance opens up a gambit of emotions that may not have been experienced in Rock and Hope’s stories. Their emotional journey and redemption is simply beautiful. One minute you’ll be grabbing your fictional baseball bat to knock some sense into them and the next you’ll be ugly crying for days. I took my time with this book because I knew I wanted to enjoy each beautiful chapter instead of speed reading my way to the end. The extra time I spent reading this slowly made the journey even more worth it. You may have broken my heart, Autumn, but by the end you stitched it slowly back together to form something more beautiful than before it was shattered. <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="14794229464073481162" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780990794561" href="/book/show/23662114-tattered-on-my-sleeve">review of another edition</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1633602676" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12427667922153346083"><blockquote>
  <b>"Nothing to be scared of, sweetheart. I got you. I'll fucking massacre anyone who tries to touch you-even a ghost."</b>
</blockquote> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1468901193i/19756509.jpg' width='' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><blockquote>
  <b>"Come stay with me."</b>
</blockquote> <b>Tattered on My Sleeve</b> is the fourth book in the Lost Kings MC. Although you can read this as a stand-alone, I do not recommend it. The characters are so intricately connected and in order to experience the full magnitude of the club, you should start with the first book in the series <b>Slow Burn</b>. The first three books focus on the club President Rock and </span>
  <span id="freeText12427667922153346083" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>"Nothing to be scared of, sweetheart. I got you. I'll fucking massacre anyone who tries to touch you-even a ghost."</b>
</blockquote> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1468901193i/19756509.jpg" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><blockquote>
  <b>"Come stay with me."</b>
</blockquote> <b>Tattered on My Sleeve</b> is the fourth book in the Lost Kings MC. Although you can read this as a stand-alone, I do not recommend it. The characters are so intricately connected and in order to experience the full magnitude of the club, you should start with the first book in the series <b>Slow Burn</b>. The first three books focus on the club President Rock and his ol' lady Hope! <b>Tattered on My Sleeve</b> is all about Wrath (the club Sergeant-at-arms) and Trinity (one of the club girls). From the first three books in the series, we know that Trinity and Wrath have quite a history together. This is their story. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1463934194i/19176817._SX540_.png" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><blockquote>
  <b>"This is perfect."</b>
</blockquote> Wyatt "Wrath" Ramsey is responsible for the security of the Brotherhood. He is all about protecting his club. When he meets the beautiful blonde bartender Trinity Hurst, a simple ride on the town on his bike ignites a flame that will be tested but never fully burns out. Wrath and Trinity share a few nights together, and the start of a relationship begins to bloom. However, when Wrath is sent out on club business, Trinity finds herself in some trouble. She calls Rock for help. When Wrath returns from his run, he finds Trinity is the new club girl for the MC. Wrath is furious, and a battle of the heart between Trinity and Wrath is waged.<blockquote>
  <b>"This is it. She's it. Stop fucking it up."</b>
</blockquote> Wrath is so broken by Trinity's willingness to serve "his club" instead of being "only his" that he pushes her far away. Although Trinity is a force to be reckoned with, her past has caused her to be cautious with men. She feels rejected by Wrath and hence, the pain begins. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1468901193i/19756510.jpg" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><blockquote>
  <b>"She's mine. I'm hers. No more fucking nonsense."</b>
</blockquote> <b>Tattered on My Sleeve</b> explores Trinity and Wrath's past and their present. The history between the two has put a barrier between them that seems indestructible. They are continuously causing each other pain. Wrath has no problem entertaining the club whores, and Trinity has found solace in the arms of the brothers. And yet, Wrath and Trinity share a bond. As the years pass, the glances, the touches, the memories, eventually sweep in and smack them both down with the force of a train. But can they truly forget the years of pain and torture they have inflicted on each other? <blockquote>
  <b>"I want her to beg for my cock. I want her to scream my name. I want her to admit that she's mine in front of everyone."</b>
</blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1468901193i/19756511.jpg" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><blockquote>
  <b>"Don't make me wait, Angel Face. I want to lick, and suck your pretty pussy until you come."</b>
</blockquote> Told in dual POV, I adored this addition to the series. The characterization was so thoroughly explored that I felt every ounce of emotion with every single solitary moment that passed. The depth of pain that Trinity endured as a child was so deep that it affected her life. That pain was so profound that she had to learn how to accept the love of a man. Wrath, the strong and loyal best friend, was so stubborn that he missed so much precious time. I loved the constant pendulum swing between "healing tenderness" and "fiery passion" shared between the two. Wrath and Trinity are perfectly matched, and I found watching the "advance/retreat" between the two invigorating as opposed to "angsty." The relationship between Wrath and Trinity also significantly affected the dynamics of the club. I thoroughly enjoyed every second of the guys and girls of the LOKI! For the Rock and Hope fans, as you know from the first three books, they are still a very critical part of the story, and you will be happy to catch an additional perspective on their relationship as well! <blockquote>
  <b>"You're mine to protect. Mine to love. Anyone hurts you, I'll kill them."</b>
</blockquote> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1463934194i/19176817._SX540_.png" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Overall, <b>Tattered on My Sleeve</b> is sheer perfection! With each book, I am more addicted to this series. The superb blend of complex characters, club dynamics, action, and passion make the Lost Kings MC a must read! Bravo Ms. Lake! Bravo!<br><br><b>***Lost Kings MC***<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23161447.Slow_Burn__Lost_Kings_MC__1_" title="Slow Burn (Lost Kings MC #1) by Autumn Jones Lake" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1410308087s/23161447.jpg" alt="Slow Burn (Lost Kings MC #1) by Autumn Jones Lake" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a <div id="review_1221545075" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1221545075" />
    <a title="Storm&#39;s Steamy Reads Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31439277-storm-s-steamy-reads-book-blog"><img alt="Storm&#39;s Steamy Reads Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1412652530p2/31439277.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1221545075?book_show_action=true">Mar 07, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Storm&#39;s Steamy Reads Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Storm&#39;s Steamy Reads Book Blog" href="/user/show/31439277-storm-s-steamy-reads-book-blog">Storm&#39;s Steamy Reads Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780990794561" href="/book/show/23662114-tattered-on-my-sleeve">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31439277-storm-s-steamy-reads-book-blog?shelf=favorites-of-all-time">favorites-of-all-time</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31439277-storm-s-steamy-reads-book-blog?shelf=best-mc">best-mc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31439277-storm-s-steamy-reads-book-blog?shelf=hot-alpha-male">hot-alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31439277-storm-s-steamy-reads-book-blog?shelf=best-of-2015">best-of-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31439277-storm-s-steamy-reads-book-blog?shelf=2015-most-anticipated">2015-most-anticipated</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31439277-storm-s-steamy-reads-book-blog?shelf=gritty">gritty</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1221545075" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17465708546435081714">5 BEAUTIFULLY TATTERED, RIP YOUR HEART OUT STARS!!<br/><br/>I’m stunned by the sincere, heartfelt intensity of Tattered on My Sleeve. I shouldn’t be. Hope and Rock’s journey was no picnic and full of struggles. Brace yourself, this author has sharpened the tools she uses to rip your heart out with Wrath and Trinity’s story. <br/><br/>We know who Trinity is. She told Hope very plainly in Corrupting Cinderella that she “serves the members on as-needed basis”. Yet, Trinity is written like no other “club girl” I’ve eve</span>
  <span id="freeText17465708546435081714" style="display:none">5 BEAUTIFULLY TATTERED, RIP YOUR HEART OUT STARS!!<br /><br />I’m stunned by the sincere, heartfelt intensity of Tattered on My Sleeve. I shouldn’t be. Hope and Rock’s journey was no picnic and full of struggles. Brace yourself, this author has sharpened the tools she uses to rip your heart out with Wrath and Trinity’s story. <br /><br />We know who Trinity is. She told Hope very plainly in Corrupting Cinderella that she “serves the members on as-needed basis”. Yet, Trinity is written like no other “club girl” I’ve ever read before. The only one who comes close is Dorothy in Madeline Sheehan’s Undeniable series. I already loved Trinity from the first three books. I thought Wrath was a big jerk who couldn’t admit he was in love with her. I expected a simple story about them finally admitting their feelings and getting together.<br /><br />I should have known better. Nothing this author does is simple. Autumn Jones Lake is not your conventional romance author. Tattered does not follow any of the usual romance formulas. But it’s a beautiful journey and ends on the perfect note. <br /><br />Wrath surpassed all my expectations for the perfect alpha hero in a romance. Biker or otherwise. He's hot and possessive. He's also understanding and forgiving. After he decides to stop fucking around, he puts Trinity's needs first, even though at times he has no idea what they are. I really fell in love with him for the way he would be gentle when she needed gentle and hard when she needed hard. <br /><br />Tattered is a long, emotional book. The author was not fucking around when she chose the title. Be prepared to cry, laugh and want to smack these two. I'm almost mad at myself for reading it too fast. I need to go back and reread!</span>
  <a data-text-id="17465708546435081714" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1239778813" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1239778813" />
    <a title="Jorja Price" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/35974976-jorja-price"><img alt="Jorja Price" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1413378753p2/35974976.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1239778813?book_show_action=true">Mar 28, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jorja Price" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jorja Price" href="/user/show/35974976-jorja-price">Jorja Price</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780990794561" href="/book/show/23662114-tattered-on-my-sleeve">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">biker romance fans, alpha male lovers</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35974976-jorja-price?shelf=best-mc-romance">best-mc-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35974976-jorja-price?shelf=the-feels">the-feels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35974976-jorja-price?shelf=could-not-put-down">could-not-put-down</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35974976-jorja-price?shelf=panty-melting">panty-melting</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35974976-jorja-price?shelf=best-alpha-male">best-alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35974976-jorja-price?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1239778813" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer872543425200483968">TATTERED ON MY SLEEVE, the 4th book in the Lost Kings MC series, starts eight years prior to Slow Burn. For the first part the book moves back and forth between the past and present with scenes that compliment each other. You’d see how they fucked up in the past and then you’d see them in a similar situation in the present where they got it right (or almost). I really loved that. It’s different and I don’t think I’ve seen very many books attempt that before.<br/><br/>I don’t want to spoil it, but because </span>
  <span id="freeText872543425200483968" style="display:none">TATTERED ON MY SLEEVE, the 4th book in the Lost Kings MC series, starts eight years prior to Slow Burn. For the first part the book moves back and forth between the past and present with scenes that compliment each other. You’d see how they fucked up in the past and then you’d see them in a similar situation in the present where they got it right (or almost). I really loved that. It’s different and I don’t think I’ve seen very many books attempt that before.<br /><br />I don’t want to spoil it, but because of the way it’s written, you are rooting for Wrath and Trinity to get their shit together from the very beginning. We are given a hint right from the start that Trinity has a dark secret in her past. The author does what so many authors can’t seem to figure out how to do. She teases the story out in a realistic way. We don’t get a big back story or info dump on page one. Nope. The story moves along and we pick up clues and learn things along the way. And when you finally learn the story, it’s devastating. By then all you want to do is hug Trinity. Has that story line been done before? Sure. Has it been done like this? NEVER.<br /><br />Wrath also has his own dark past. It shaped him into who he is, but he’s not some whiny, angsty guy who wallows in the past. He feels deeply and you really see his caring side without the author completely emmasculating him. I don’t know what it is, but this author knows how to write fierce alpha male characters who are also deep, and sensitive in their own way, without making them pussies. REAL MEN. Not violent assholes who pretend to be men. Wrath is no exception. He is who he is and doesn’t give a fuck what anyone thinks of him. <br /><br />What fascinated me about Tattered is how closely woven and interconnected it is to the first three books, yet it is not just a retelling of those stories. When events overlap, they are told from Wrath’s or Trinity’s side and how it impacts them. You learn Wrath often wasn’t being the big jerk everyone thought he was. My favorite thing is the layers and deep feelings explored between all of the characters. Rock and Wrath’s relationship has always been one of my favorites. But seeing things from Wrath’s side makes you look at Rock a little…different. Not bad different. Wrath loves Rock and looks up to him very much like a big brother. But he’s also incredibly angry and frustrated with him (with good reason). My other favorite relationship is between Wrath and Hope. They provide some needed comic relief! Besides their funny moments, they also share some deep ones. <br /><br />We already saw how Wrath’s attitude towards Hope changed over the first three books, but now we see it from his perspective and it made me love him even more. Like Rock, Wrath treats the women around the MC with respect, even if he dislikes them. He’s not abusive to prove he’s a “real man”. One of my favorite scenes is when he throws Cookie out of the clubhouse. He’s firm but not mean or cruel and when she’s blubbering about what she should do, he simply says “leave.”<br /><br />We also get to see his relationship with the other brothers—and Wrath’s immense patience and restraint. Z – the prankster. Murphy and Teller who are young and dumb. We also get to see more of the brothers that we’ve only heard bits and pieces from. Ravage, Dex, Stash and Sparky make a few appearances. <br /><br />I loved every page of Tattered on My Sleeve and I can't wait for more from the Lost Kings MC. I'm really hoping the author does another book with Wrath and Trinity and Hope and Rock. I'm also looking forward to Murphy and Heidi's story (or Axel and Heidi the suspense is killing me!).<br /><br />If you're looking for a fast, quick, smutty read, this isn't your book. Tattered On My Sleeve is intense, deep, emotional, and burning hot. It will break your heart, melt your panties and leave you with a big smile on your face when it's over.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="872543425200483968" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1339471198?book_show_action=true">Jul 19, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17972955006102236414">★★★★ <b>4 Stars</b> ★★★★<br/><br/><b>Now LIVE!<br/>US <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://bit.ly/LKMC4_WRATH'>http://bit.ly/LKMC4_WRATH</a> <br/>UK - <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://bit.ly/LKMC4_Wrath_UK'>http://bit.ly/LKMC4_Wrath_UK</a></b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437750110i/15625285._SY540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Do you know what, it's about damn time someone wrote a book about a heroine who is as 'slutty' as her male counterpart. Tattered on my Sleeve is basically a second chance romance between Sergeant-at- Arms, Wyatt 'Wrath' Ramsey, and club Mama, Trinity Hirst.<br/><br/>Trinity grew up in the MC life and has literally seen it all, she's experienced things that would break most people and have leave a long lasting psycholog</span>
  <span id="freeText17972955006102236414" style="display:none">★★★★ <b>4 Stars</b> ★★★★<br><br><b>Now LIVE!<br>US <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://bit.ly/LKMC4_WRATH">http://bit.ly/LKMC4_WRATH</a> <br>UK - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://bit.ly/LKMC4_Wrath_UK">http://bit.ly/LKMC4_Wrath_UK</a></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437750110i/15625285._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Do you know what, it's about damn time someone wrote a book about a heroine who is as 'slutty' as her male counterpart. Tattered on my Sleeve is basically a second chance romance between Sergeant-at- Arms, Wyatt 'Wrath' Ramsey, and club Mama, Trinity Hirst.<br><br>Trinity grew up in the MC life and has literally seen it all, she's experienced things that would break most people and have leave a long lasting psychological effect. However, she is a very strong woman, and when the President of The Lost Kings MC offers her shelter and protection she is so grateful that she ends up making the club her life. She takes pride in looking after the compound and all of the brothers, and although she is never obliged to, she does indulge in recreational sex, and why the hell not!<br><br>There is one problem though, and that comes in the form of the blond haired and beautiful, underground fighter, and Sergeant-at- Arms, -Wrath.<br><br>In a case of bad timing, they meet the week before Trinity's past catches up with her, and they have beautiful 3 days together before Wrath has to go on a run. Trinity feels strangely safe with this big bad biker and he is drawn to her sweet and fearless charm.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"She glared up at me with bold eyes.<br>Her fearlessness was the biggest turn-on."</b>
</blockquote><br>The shit hits the fan and a man from her past spots her which causes her to seek help from Wrath's president at The Lost Kings. On his return, Wrath begs her to not move into the clubhouse, but she has no choice.<br><br>Wrath assumes that she is offering herself up to his brothers, so refuses to listen to her explanation and for eight years they torture each other by going with other people and their relationship becomes a destructive one.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>I'm too fucked up.<br>Too damaged to ever be anything more than I am now.<br>A club whore."</b>
</blockquote><br>When Wrath finally comes to his senses, he realises that he needs to claim this beautiful and kind hearted woman.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437750208i/15625305._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>_ _ _ _<br><br>Autumn Jones Lake is a new author to me, I have not read the first 3 books in this series which follow the President's journey to find love. This was not an easy read, it was such a detailed story, spanning 8 years and the character development and story progression was phenomenal.<br><br>Wyatt was your typical biker, he had his share of club sluts and was absolutely awful to Trinity at times, but I can forgive my fictitious bikers because as much as Wyatt was lashing out in anger, deep down he was a passionate and loyal man who had a delicious alpha possessive vibe going on for his girl.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"Holy fuck.<br>We're so goddamn dysfunctional and twisted. I don't know if I can ever fix us.<br>But I want to try."</b>
</blockquote><br>My heart broke for poor Trinity, she was trying to make the best of her life after a horrific start and I could absolutely forgive her for using sex as both a weapon and a crutch. Since her daddy died when she was a child she hadn't received or given love and truly believed that her only value was for sex, I found it so sad.<br><br>I loved how everybody loved and appreciated her and that it was Wrath who finally made her see and believe that just because she had sex with a lot of the men in the brotherhood, that she was a woman with compassion, a talent for art, and many other attributes that made her, her. She was worth everything.<br><br>The writing was flawless, and I think if it wasn't as long as it was (sorry, I'm not a fan of mega long books) then I would have rate slightly higher. I am looking forward to future books in this series which will concentrate on new characters but also catch up with the previous ones.<br><br><b>This is a standalone biker romance, told in dual POV, past and present. </b><br><br><i>ARC gratefully received from the author in exchange for an honest review</i><br><br><a href="http://ilovebooklove-ab.blogspot.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420460638i/13228252.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420460638i/13228250.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<span id="freeTextContainer10664576113324190809">This was a long one but so worth it!! I have never read an MC book that was so detailed and complicated. This book is raw, gritty, emotional and heart-breaking.<br/>It's the story of Wrath and Trinity. Trinity is a woman who's been raised in motorcycle clubs. She knows bikers well and she knows her way around them. Wrath is the sergeant-at-arms of The Lost Kings MC. He is cocky, a player and he never plans to settle down, let alone have an old lady. Everything changes when he meets Trinity at one of </span>
  <span id="freeText10664576113324190809" style="display:none">This was a long one but so worth it!! I have never read an MC book that was so detailed and complicated. This book is raw, gritty, emotional and heart-breaking.<br>It's the story of Wrath and Trinity. Trinity is a woman who's been raised in motorcycle clubs. She knows bikers well and she knows her way around them. Wrath is the sergeant-at-arms of The Lost Kings MC. He is cocky, a player and he never plans to settle down, let alone have an old lady. Everything changes when he meets Trinity at one of the club's bars. Her personality is like a shock of fresh air and he is immediately captivated. Trinity is attracted to him as well but her low self-esteem makes her doubt herself. <br><br><br><a href="http://s1260.photobucket.com/user/linalove1988/media/11781797_963267347066829_5893016652905476627_n_zps2oyusbvf.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437981710i/15652734._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 11781797_963267347066829_5893016652905476627_n_zps2oyusbvf.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1260.photobucket.com/user/linalove1988/media/11751964_963266237066940_4636137135031079554_n_zpsgpkbubrz.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437981710i/15652736._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 11751964_963266237066940_4636137135031079554_n_zpsgpkbubrz.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>They begin a short but very passionate affair that comes to an abrupt end when Trinity's past comes back to haunt her. <br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1260.photobucket.com/user/linalove1988/media/10985353_963266463733584_19324359586678353_n_zps1ouldffc.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437982019i/15652754._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 10985353_963266463733584_19324359586678353_n_zps1ouldffc.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br><br>Trinity is forced to make a choice and that choice will push Wrath out of her life. Being a club mama means that she is fair game to anyone of the brothers. Wrath's stubborn personality won't let her explain that her life is in danger and so, they begin a push and pull relationship that will ruin them. Wrath's jealousy against his president and his club brothers will poison his feelings for Trinity and they will spend eight years trying to destroy and hurt each other.<br><br><br>Their lives will be shaken from that short affair and they will have to face each other every day while forcing themselves to be apart. They will lose themselves into a useless chain of affairs that has only one purpose; to make the other one hurt.<br>The road to happiness is built with thorns and the way to forgiveness will be rocky and dangerous. One thing is for certain; they need each other.<br><br><a href="http://s1260.photobucket.com/user/linalove1988/media/11745940_963265707066993_1138664696744899618_n_zps4qwyynm3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437981710i/15652735._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 11745940_963265707066993_1138664696744899618_n_zps4qwyynm3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The book was a long one. It could have been really tiring if the writing and heroes weren't so great. The book was very detailed and there were a lot of characters that made it richer. I was amazed because I wasn't tired at all while I was reading it. It's one hell of a long ride, but you will not be disappointed. If you love MC books you will love this one. I highly recommend it and now I am very curious about the other books in the series.<br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><b>5 Magnificent Stars from me!<br><br>Release Date: July 28th</b><br><i>I received an ARC in exchange for an honest review.</i></span>

<div id="review_1178128952" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1178128952" />
    <a title="Iza" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9263805-iza"><img alt="Iza" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600025009p2/9263805.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1178128952?book_show_action=true">Jan 23, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Iza" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Iza" href="/user/show/9263805-iza">Iza</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/25674863-tattered-on-my-sleeve">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1178128952" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11480396881413716857">Another I've waited many months for. I do have the knack of falling for side characters. And Wrath was no exception.<br/><br/>Of course that, at first, I didn't like him. He was an a-hole to Hope and Trinity, too. I don't know where and when, but that changed and I became #PropertyofWrath. I kept bugging Autumn about it, but she's so awesome and a sweetie, being patient with me and not getting mad. What can I say, I'm passionate about characters I love!<br/><br/>"I don't get on my knees for anyone. Ever."<br/><br/>We've all </span>
  <span id="freeText11480396881413716857" style="display:none">Another I've waited many months for. I do have the knack of falling for side characters. And Wrath was no exception.<br /><br />Of course that, at first, I didn't like him. He was an a-hole to Hope and Trinity, too. I don't know where and when, but that changed and I became #PropertyofWrath. I kept bugging Autumn about it, but she's so awesome and a sweetie, being patient with me and not getting mad. What can I say, I'm passionate about characters I love!<br /><br />"I don't get on my knees for anyone. Ever."<br /><br />We've all met Trinity in the previous books. She's the woman in charge of running the club house; cleaning, cooking. She's also a club momma. Now, the fact that a woman sleeps with men she likes, whenever she likes is not a big deal. However, in the MC world, there's no respect for women that do that. Outside of the LOKI MC, there was no respect for Trin. Of course that Rock's a sweetheart and has laid down the law, from the beginning. It was her choice.<br /><br />Now, at first, I was pissed at Trinity. I didn't get it. She frustrated me to no end. I ached for Wrath. But, as the story progressed, we found out more and more and I started to understand, and really, it broke my heart. We all have a past. Some of us had it better than others. Trin was in the latter. <br /><br />Wrath had his moments too. He'd piss me off - there's proof of that in a convo with Autumn, hah - then he'd say or do something and make me melt. Both of them are so complex and complicated but they make it work. Once they overcome some things - cough, Wrath pulls his head out of his lovely derriere, cough - all's well. Or, as can be expected in the MC world. <br /><br />The many feelings I've had ranged from being pissed, frustrated, to teary-eyed, brokenhearted and wanting more. Yes, it's a long book but I still want more. It's Wrath, can you blame me? I loved it. I'm going to reread it, I'm sure of that.<br /><br />It was one heck of a ride. 5 stars.<br /><br />I wish to thank the author and Give Me Books for this copy given in exchange of an honest review.<br /><br />P.S. Wrath is also #PropertyofIza. </span>
  <a data-text-id="11480396881413716857" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1227501976" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1227501976" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1227501976?book_show_action=true">Mar 14, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rosa Sharon (iScream Books Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rosa Sharon (iScream Books Blog)" href="/user/show/16932050-rosa-sharon-iscream-books-blog">Rosa Sharon (iScream Books Blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780990794561" href="/book/show/23662114-tattered-on-my-sleeve">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16932050-rosa-sharon-iscream-books-blog?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16932050-rosa-sharon-iscream-books-blog?shelf=badass">badass</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16932050-rosa-sharon-iscream-books-blog?shelf=badass-biker-alert">badass-biker-alert</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16932050-rosa-sharon-iscream-books-blog?shelf=dirty-talkin">dirty-talkin</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16932050-rosa-sharon-iscream-books-blog?shelf=multiple-pov">multiple-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16932050-rosa-sharon-iscream-books-blog?shelf=suspense">suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16932050-rosa-sharon-iscream-books-blog?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16932050-rosa-sharon-iscream-books-blog?shelf=call-the-fire-dept-hot">call-the-fire-dept-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16932050-rosa-sharon-iscream-books-blog?shelf=copy-for-review">copy-for-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16932050-rosa-sharon-iscream-books-blog?shelf=female-badass">female-badass</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1227501976" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10188694348378549775"><b>
  <i>Dysfunctional and twisted...</i>
</b><br/><br/>I've been anxiously waiting to get my hands on Wrath. Well, yes, I would love to touch his "muscle-y-male perfection", but I meant his book. He captured my heart when his softened towards 'Cinderella' in the previous book. That's when I knew that he had the promise of being an incredible main character and I wanted to get to know him better. I had also gotten glimpses of the chemistry and tension between Wrath and Trinity and wondered what their story was. It was </span>
  <span id="freeText10188694348378549775" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>Dysfunctional and twisted...</i>
</b><br /><br />I've been anxiously waiting to get my hands on Wrath. Well, yes, I would love to touch his "muscle-y-male perfection", but I meant his book. He captured my heart when his softened towards 'Cinderella' in the previous book. That's when I knew that he had the promise of being an incredible main character and I wanted to get to know him better. I had also gotten glimpses of the chemistry and tension between Wrath and Trinity and wondered what their story was. It was a much longer story than I expected, you will get your money's worth when you one-click for sure.<br /> <br />Their beginning was so perfect. They connected instantly and their chemistry was so strong that their was no denying it. She was funny and sassy, not taking shit from anyone. I thought she was perfect for Wrath, whom she tagged as 'Wrecking Ball' due to his Sergeant-at-arms position with the Lost Kings MC. I was excited as I felt their passion and enjoyed their banter. It wasn't until it all fell apart that I remembered having met Trinity before, that she was the girl that befriended Hope at the clubhouse. So, now I'm finally understanding that I've gone back in time and that this story is running parallel to Rock &amp; Hope's story. I'm getting a new perspective of some of the events that were previously covered and it's very enlightening. I fell even more in love with Wrath as his layers were peeled back and his heart was exposed. He is the muscle of the club, the protector, the enforcer. He's huge, with rippling muscles and a sexy smirk that keeps the women lined up for a chance with him. He's always taken advantage of that and never desired more than instant gratification...<i>
  <b>until her.</b>
</i><br /> <br />Trinity is broken. Her past is painful and has bled into her future, keeping her expectations low and her dreams disturbed. When an event takes place that causes her to seek out the club's protection lines get crossed and misunderstandings take place. She's thrown into his life, whether he likes it or not, and he can't escape the pull he feels towards her. She's like a magnet to his metal and it's a constant battle to fight their chemistry, but unfortunately he's very strong and fight he does. Not only in the clubhouse but in the gym and the ring. That's where he takes his frustration and anger, further enhancing that perfect eight-pack that has all the women drooling. Yes, Trinity is one of them, but she keeps her drooling to herself. She admires him from afar, keeping her distance, feeling the pain as she sees those women coming and going. It's painful for her to witness because she knows exactly what she's missing, how good it was, what she might have had..<b>
  <i>if only.</i>
</b><br /> <br />Get ready to melt and sigh, to gasp and giggle, and to yearn and yell as you experience the desperation and danger of yet another amazing installment in the Lost Kings MC series. I love how the author describes the endings as HFN, which stands for Happy For Now, because 'thank goodness' their story is not over. We still have Teller, Murphy, Axel, Z and who knows how many other "brothers by choice" to keep us coming back for more for a long time to come.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10188694348378549775" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1229128952" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1229128952" />
    <a title="Sheila" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/39321386-sheila"><img alt="Sheila" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1521765588p2/39321386.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1229128952?book_show_action=true">Mar 16, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sheila" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sheila" href="/user/show/39321386-sheila">Sheila</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/25674863-tattered-on-my-sleeve">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1229128952" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2266011278049977926">I received an ARC in exchange for an honest review.<br/><br/>Wow. This way more than your typical MC romance. Wrath and Trinity had hurt one another in ways most couples I know could never recover from. They both will have to constantly forgive and try to forget with painful reminders being in their faces every single day. It won't be easy, but as this book so incontrovertibly proves to us, the devotion they have to each other is strong enough to pull them through. <br/><br/>Trinity's story is brutally painful and </span>
  <span id="freeText2266011278049977926" style="display:none">I received an ARC in exchange for an honest review.<br /><br />Wow. This way more than your typical MC romance. Wrath and Trinity had hurt one another in ways most couples I know could never recover from. They both will have to constantly forgive and try to forget with painful reminders being in their faces every single day. It won't be easy, but as this book so incontrovertibly proves to us, the devotion they have to each other is strong enough to pull them through. <br /><br />Trinity's story is brutally painful and even though I know the last thing she would want is pity I couldn't help but feel sorry for the Trinity of her childhood. Experiences that would've broken anyone else only made her more determined to rise above. Her feelings of low self-worth are evidence that although she survived she didn't escape unscathed. Each time she thought to herself that she wasn't anything but a 'club whore' it broke a piece of my heart.<br /><br />Wrath's love for her just kept surprising me over and over again. I would think I knew how deep his feelings ran then he would say or do something else that expressed an even deeper level of unconditional love. It required unfailing persistence and patience to finally break through the walls she had built to protect herself and truly believe he felt the way he said he did.<br /><br />All of the club brothers surprised me with their love and support of Trinity. All those years she had been living under their protection she never considered she was anything more than a sexual outlet for them. The protective barriers she had erected around her heart didn't allow her to see that they considered her their friend, and more than one admitted to having had stronger feelings for her that went beyond a physical relationship but they didn't think they'd ever have a chance with her so didn't try. Wrath is the one who stood up and fought for her as his girl, even if it was eight years later than it should've been they both just want to put the past behind them and work on their new future.<br /><br />This book takes place along the same timeline as books one through three, so we see the same events we've read about before, just from another viewpoint. The character development in these books is exceedingly complex, even for the supporting characters. I can't wait for Z's story, as well as Murphy, Teller and Heidi's! I'm already passionate about each of them and feel like I know them personally and they've never even been the sole focus of a book yet.<br /><br />This is honestly one of the best MC series I've ever read. If you enjoy a dirty talking, protective and devoted alpha then these are for you!<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2266011278049977926" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1314743508" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1314743508" />
    <a title="Mandie Foxylutely" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3863513-mandie-foxylutely"><img alt="Mandie Foxylutely" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1517252649p2/3863513.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1314743508?book_show_action=true">Jun 22, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mandie Foxylutely" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mandie Foxylutely" href="/user/show/3863513-mandie-foxylutely">Mandie Foxylutely</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780990794561" href="/book/show/23662114-tattered-on-my-sleeve">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3863513-mandie-foxylutely?shelf=erotics">erotics</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3863513-mandie-foxylutely?shelf=alpha-kick-ass-mofos">alpha-kick-ass-mofos</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3863513-mandie-foxylutely?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3863513-mandie-foxylutely?shelf=absorbfest">absorbfest</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3863513-mandie-foxylutely?shelf=angst">angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3863513-mandie-foxylutely?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3863513-mandie-foxylutely?shelf=insecurities">insecurities</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3863513-mandie-foxylutely?shelf=we-need-to-talk-you-bastard-moments">we-need-to-talk-you-bastard-moments</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3863513-mandie-foxylutely?shelf=bikers">bikers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3863513-mandie-foxylutely?shelf=mc">mc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1314743508" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15674164442601543674">This is the fourth book in the Lost Kings MC series and although this can be read independent I would advise to read the previous books as reference to what has happened in those will appear throughout this book. This is Wrath and Trinity’s story which begins eight years prior to the series start and we finally get to see what had happened between this feisty couple which we had had glimpses of in Rock and Hope’s story.<br/><br/>The story is unravelled with the back story interwoven to present day so the </span>
  <span id="freeText15674164442601543674" style="display:none">This is the fourth book in the Lost Kings MC series and although this can be read independent I would advise to read the previous books as reference to what has happened in those will appear throughout this book. This is Wrath and Trinity’s story which begins eight years prior to the series start and we finally get to see what had happened between this feisty couple which we had had glimpses of in Rock and Hope’s story.<br /><br />The story is unravelled with the back story interwoven to present day so the reader is taken on a journey to understand the complex and frustrating path that Wrath and Trinity have been on. Both are holding back on past issues that have made them hold onto their outer protective shell that can give off conflicting imagery of who they are.<br /><br />Trinity has lead a troubled life but she thought when she met Wrath that day she felt a connection that gave her hope for the future. Wrath felt the same but something happens for that chance of a love to blossom to be firmly pushed back leading to eight years of misunderstandings, hurts and the constant playing against each other to hold onto their selfish pride.<br /><br />This was an in depth and emotive read but I just kept routing for these two to actually sit down and talk to each other. It took a long time and further issues thrown in but once we get to the revelations it was just engrossing to watch all that play out.<br /><br />I have always routed for Trinity. This beautiful and gentle soul who has only ever thought she was raised for one role in her life and to never be able to be loved for who she is. When she felt cast aside by Wrath, my heart just melted for her. I loved how strong she became in this book and showed her true colours and confidence.<br /><br />As for Wrath, well I have always loved this gorgeous, abrupt alpha man. The tough fighter who is also the SAA for the MC (aka The Wrecking Ball!) was underneath a sweet and loving man. When first reading about him in the first books, he comes off as a bit of a bully and antagonistic. But it wasn’t until reading this book from his and Trinity’s POV that you get to see the other side and understand the reason he said this or did that. He wasn’t being a dick when he was saying those things to Hope, he was opening her eyes and making sure she understood what being part of the MC would be for her.<br /><br />The chemistry and passion between Wrath and Trinity was so sensual, erotic and HOT! I found myself having to fan myself down when this man and his clever tongue got going (in more ways than one!) I loved it when Trinity called him by his real name (and no I won’t reveal it here)<br /><br />The secondary characters of the men in the MC were further developed and new ones included. It was good to see more of Teller, Murphy and Z plus meet Ravage, Dex, Sparky and Stash. I also can’t wait for Axel to get his cut!<br /><br />At times I did wonder where the book would take us to as it was a very long storyline to get through (hey we had a lot of years to cover!) but I was a bit surprised by the ending and I was left drooling for more which I guess is a very good way to leave a reader - at a HFN. Happily there are more books to come with further coverage of Wrath, Hope and Rock, oh and I just can’t wait to find out more about the Murphy, Heidi and Axel love triangle! Five LOKI is the best stars!<br /><br /><i>*ARC kindly provided by the author in exchange for an honest review</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="15674164442601543674" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shawna  Wood (A Girl and Her Books)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shawna  Wood (A Girl and Her Books)" href="/user/show/37390860-shawna-wood-a-girl-and-her-books">Shawna  Wood (A Girl and Her Books)</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1342804504" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15904265263349772393">I have one word for this book, WOW! I was obsessed with Trinity and Wrath story. Every free moment I had I was reading their story and hoping they could make it work. <br/><br/>Trinity and Wrath are two very broken people. They each have suffered abuse at the hands of the people they trusted most. Trinity in particular has suffered through heinous abuse that has left her soul scarred. Trinity has let these scares define who she is, which puts prevents her from having any meaning relationships. <br/><br/>When Trinit</span>
  <span id="freeText15904265263349772393" style="display:none">I have one word for this book, WOW! I was obsessed with Trinity and Wrath story. Every free moment I had I was reading their story and hoping they could make it work. <br /><br />Trinity and Wrath are two very broken people. They each have suffered abuse at the hands of the people they trusted most. Trinity in particular has suffered through heinous abuse that has left her soul scarred. Trinity has let these scares define who she is, which puts prevents her from having any meaning relationships. <br /><br />When Trinity meets Wrath there is an instant connection and they are two lost souls that found a home in each other. However, Trinity is unable to comprehend that a man could see her as anything more than a toy to be played with and ends up sabotaging this new relationship.<br /><br />Autumn Jones Lake throughout this series, especially in this book has, is a master of showing the beauty in the broken and ugly. Trinity and Wrath are both broken and both have an ugly past but this only defines them if they allow. I loved how this book showed that no matter what a person has been through doesn't mean they are not deserving of love and respect. <br /><br />Wrath surprised me in this book. I wasn't necessary his biggest fan, but after this book I love him. Wrath really has a big heart and the things he did for Trinity in this book had me swooning. The length he went to for Trinity was A-MA-Zing and made me fall in love with him a bit more. <br /><br />I was gifted a book for my honest review. </span>
  <a data-text-id="15904265263349772393" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">adults who understand real relationships are messy</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36976119-joy?shelf=best-of">best-of</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36976119-joy?shelf=real-romance">real-romance</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1239827480" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11644867980836366750">Beautiful story about two broken people overcoming their terrible upbringings and changing to be better for one another. I adored both Wrath and Trinity and their struggles. Trinity was flawed, broken and felt she was unworthy. Her story broke my heart. The way Wrath loves her and tries so hard to understand her was nothing short of heroic. <br/>Tattered is gritty and a departure from the author's previous books in this series, so be warned. </span>

          </span>

    <a title="Keeana Bookalicious Babes Blog " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30633574-keeana-bookalicious-babes-blog"><img alt="Keeana Bookalicious Babes Blog " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1397771311p2/30633574.jpg" /></a>
