<div id="review_2758086566" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2758086566" />
    <a title="NAT.orious reads ☾" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/54624224-nat-orious-reads"><img alt="NAT.orious reads ☾" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1606165351p2/54624224.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2758086566?book_show_action=true">Mar 24, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="NAT.orious reads ☾" class="user" itemprop="url" name="NAT.orious reads ☾" href="/user/show/54624224-nat-orious-reads">NAT.orious reads ☾</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2758086566" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9483562483621448049"><b>4 tattered ★★★★✩</b><br/><i>
  <blockquote><b>This book is for you if… </b>you are a Loki sister (or brother or even both- we don't discriminate)</blockquote>
</i><br/><b>⤐ <i>Overall.</i></b><br/>Oh my God, can this Series please never end. Right now I am still sooo wrapped up in the story that I can't even get it together for a proper review, but I will try nonetheless. That Wrath and Trin would have their own story was obvious from the moment Autumn introduced them to us in <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/41726841.Slow_Burn__Lost_Kings_MC___1_' title='Slow Burn (Lost Kings MC, #1) by Autumn Jones Lake' rel='nofollow noopener'>Slow Burn</a>. The sparks between them, as violent and hurtful as they may be from time to tim</span>
  <span id="freeText9483562483621448049" style="display:none"><b>4 tattered ★★★★✩</b><br /><i>
  <blockquote><b>This book is for you if… </b>you are a Loki sister (or brother or even both- we don't discriminate)</blockquote>
</i><br /><b>⤐ <i>Overall.</i></b><br />Oh my God, can this Series please never end. Right now I am still sooo wrapped up in the story that I can't even get it together for a proper review, but I will try nonetheless. That Wrath and Trin would have their own story was obvious from the moment Autumn introduced them to us in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/41726841.Slow_Burn__Lost_Kings_MC___1_" title="Slow Burn (Lost Kings MC, #1) by Autumn Jones Lake" rel="nofollow noopener">Slow Burn</a>. The sparks between them, as violent and hurtful as they may be from time to time, cannot be denied. But the painful past between them and the darkness that Trinity is carrying around seem to make it very hard to overcome the difficulties between them. Setting aside the not quite realistic setting of an MC, I really enjoy discovering this universe with every new book. I am glad I came across this series a couple of months ago!<br /><br /><b>⤐ <i>What’s happening.</i></b><br />Trinity has a fucked-up childhood. Her dad, an MC member had to go to prison when she was very young. The second he left their house, her good-for-nothing mother chased other guys from many MCs only procuring disaster. At first, little Trin can all but wait for her dad to come back from prison, but club business eventually takes him away from her forever. Lost is his protection and lost are the times where Trinity still had hope. Because when you turn 16 and have tits and an MC prez has his eyes on you - horrors are about to come down. After 2 years of the most horrible experiences, she finally breaks loose. And all but crashes head over heels into big scary biker guy Wrath. And suddenly, feelings come to life she can't even translate into words.<br /><br />Wrath sees Trinity and knows she is special. Their time together doesn't end with a one-night-stand, like it usually does for them with other people. After three dates both feel a special connection growing but then Trinity's past catches up and it all goes down the river from thereon. A misunderstanding, combined with Wrath's big mouth and act-before-you-think attitude and Trin's thick head, lead to 8 years of hurting each other and suffering from the consequences. Their own private war has cost them so much it seems impossible that they might trust each other ever again.<br /><br />I think seeing Rock trying to find happiness with his Baby Doll Hope makes Wrath realize that there is more to living than trying to get back at someone. And he decides that it is time to make peace. He approaches Trinity and they seem to get it together - I mean, I would try my best if I could end up with that hot fella in bed *smirk*.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9483562483621448049" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

With so many MC romances cropping up I have been a bit wary though some are good, some are so far fetched and unrealistic (me knowing what a real MC is like) that I have somewhat been avoiding them.   <span id="freeText3645126684662092014" style="display:none">A Total Must Read!<br />This is my first read by this author. With so many MC romances cropping up I have been a bit wary though some are good, some are so far fetched and unrealistic (me knowing what a real MC is like) that I have somewhat been avoiding them. The blurb for this one sounded so good though and it was recommended by a friend. Then there is the fact that this is fourth in the series and my mind balks at starting a series after the first, but I charged ahead and found myself loving this book. The author has done a great job, her writing is really resounding. I didn't feel at all at a loss at not having read the first 3 in the series although now I am definitely going to be one-clicking the others! I have to admit that the hot tattooed bikers are a definite plus. I mean who doesn't love muscular, tattooed hotties? Then there is Wrath and Trinity, the pair just totally made me swoon. It's a shame about all of this time lost between the pair because of their complete stubbornness, and totally lack of communication and a misunderstanding, but I am a totally sucker for second chances and this one is awesome. I definitely recommend! I was given a complimentary copy of this book in exchange for an honest review. </span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1218036171" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1218036171" />
    <a title="No" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/32001200-no"><img alt="No" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1425477538p2/32001200.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1218036171?book_show_action=true">Mar 04, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="No" class="user" itemprop="url" name="No" href="/user/show/32001200-no">No</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780990794561" href="/book/show/23662114-tattered-on-my-sleeve">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Mature Adults</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32001200-no?shelf=most-wanted-romance-2014">most-wanted-romance-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32001200-no?shelf=hottest-mc-romances">hottest-mc-romances</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32001200-no?shelf=panty-melter">panty-melter</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32001200-no?shelf=sexiest-alpha-male">sexiest-alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32001200-no?shelf=2015-most-wanted">2015-most-wanted</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32001200-no?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32001200-no?shelf=dominant">dominant</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32001200-no?shelf=real-life-romance">real-life-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32001200-no?shelf=rape-survivor">rape-survivor</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1218036171" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16578977596426577625"><b>Warning:</b> This is not a "typical" romance. It's not even a typical MC Romance. It is <i>extremely</i> different from the first three books in many ways, but also similar in many ways. Wrath and Trinity's story is a heart-breaking, soul-crushing, tear-your-heart-into-pieces story. It’s intense, raw, frustrating and sometimes dark. It doesn’t happen overnight. It's an epic love story about the irrational things we do when we're younger, the things we do because we don't know any better, maturing, growing,</span>
  <span id="freeText16578977596426577625" style="display:none"><b>Warning:</b> This is not a "typical" romance. It's not even a typical MC Romance. It is <i>extremely</i> different from the first three books in many ways, but also similar in many ways. Wrath and Trinity's story is a heart-breaking, soul-crushing, tear-your-heart-into-pieces story. It’s intense, raw, frustrating and sometimes dark. It doesn’t happen overnight. It's an epic love story about the irrational things we do when we're younger, the things we do because we don't know any better, maturing, growing, moving past a horrible upbringing to become a better person and most important, forgiveness. Wrath and Trinity grow and mature throughout the book, but not without a lot of hurt, anger, and heartache over the span of eight years. <br /><br />I will say even though Tattered covers a lot of heavy, emotional topics, the author does a good job of lacing humor (sometimes dark) throughout the book, so it's not in any way a depressing read. But I think you have to be a mature adult to understand this book.<br /><br />**May be considered spoilers**<br />Trinity grew up in an abusive Motorcycle Club. The horrors she endured left her with no self-esteem and many emotional scars. But she's strong enough to survive and sweet enough that she wants to help and take care of others. <br /><br />Trinity is portrayed as a <b>realistic</b> sexual abuse survivor. Unfortunately, that means she's not always <i>likeable</i>. You don't understand why she does the things she does and it's easy to label her a "slut". Once you understand why she is the way she is, you want to hug her and kick anyone's ass who talks trash about her. She has sex to feel good about herself because she thinks that's all she has to offer. That message was etched in her soul from a young age. She's not capable of making an emotional connection with her lovers.<br /><br />Enter Wrath. A force of nature. Big, bad, scary. But he recognizes the hurt Trinity carries with her and likes her for who she is. Of course Trinity can't understand that at the time. When old threats surface, she's terrified and she retreats to the behavior she knows. People have categorized it as a mere misunderstanding that pushes Wrath and Trinity apart, but it's more than that. Neither of them are mature enough to handle the much bigger issues ingrained in them. <br /><br />So for eight years they sort of co-exist. They torture each other. They act childish. They are the sum of their upbringings.<br /><br />When Wrath sees how serious his best friend and "big brother" Rock is about Hope, it wakes him up a little. Trinity's the only woman he's ever wanted. When he realizes he's the only one she's ever let her guard down with...it's explosive. But she's still got the heavy baggage of her past. When Wrath finally learns what those issues are (and by the way I wanted to kick Rock at this point-although we had a hint he was involved because he tells Hope in Strength From Loyalty that Wrath and Trinity's issues are partially his fault) he MANS THE FUCK UP and goes after Trinity relentlessly. Not just her body. Her mind and her heart too. He works hard (really hard!) to make her understand she's worth more and means more to him than "a couple of holes to stick [his] dick in." Yes, he's crude, he is after all a biker.<br /><br />Watching Trinity grow and change because of Wrath's love was a beautiful journey. The sex is panty-melting hot. But what was beautiful was seeing Trinity finally make the connection between love, sex and emotion. At one point, she has an a-ha! moment when she's out with Hope and some guy hits on her. Normally she would have just had sex with him, but she knows Wrath's waiting at home for her and she can't wait to go home to him. That was one of my favorite parts because you really saw her growing and changing her mindset there.<br /><br />Tattered is a long, tear-filled journey. Trinity is not magically "healed" by the end. Neither of them are (Wrath has his own emotional scars). But they are committed to working TOGETHER because they love each other. I really hope we get another book about them in the future.<br /><br />I guess my <b>only</b> complaint would be that Trinity never gets therapy of any kind. Her healing all comes at the hands of the hero making her whole again and while that is incredibly <i>romantic</i>, it's not, <i>realistic</i> at all. I think someone as damaged as Trinity would still need counseling and a lot of help to recover fully.<br /><br />But this is fiction, not real life So I still give it 5 beautifully broken stars.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16578977596426577625" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1340427647" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1340427647" />
    <a title="Michelle Brace (Wicked Babes Blog Reviews)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9200399-michelle-brace-wicked-babes-blog-reviews"><img alt="Michelle Brace (Wicked Babes Blog Reviews)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1436158044p2/9200399.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1340427647?book_show_action=true">Jul 20, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle Brace (Wicked Babes Blog Reviews)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle Brace (Wicked Babes Blog Reviews)" href="/user/show/9200399-michelle-brace-wicked-babes-blog-reviews">Michelle Brace (Wicked Babes Blog Reviews)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780990794561" href="/book/show/23662114-tattered-on-my-sleeve">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1340427647" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12253230127184119590">All I can say is WOW! I have never read a book by Autumn and I am so glad that I read this one. I will definitely be reading the others in this series for sure. She knocked it out of the ball park with this one. I am in LOVE with Wrath and Trinity. I was so hooked on this book that time flew and before I knew it, it was 3 a.m. and I was forced to put it down grudgingly. I don't like spoilers so I won't go into too much detail but you need to pick this book up. It was so, so good.<br/><br/>This book is abo</span>
  <span id="freeText12253230127184119590" style="display:none">All I can say is WOW! I have never read a book by Autumn and I am so glad that I read this one. I will definitely be reading the others in this series for sure. She knocked it out of the ball park with this one. I am in LOVE with Wrath and Trinity. I was so hooked on this book that time flew and before I knew it, it was 3 a.m. and I was forced to put it down grudgingly. I don't like spoilers so I won't go into too much detail but you need to pick this book up. It was so, so good.<br /><br />This book is about the relationship between Trinity and Wrath and all the twist and turns that they went through. In the beginning they were going good until Wrath had to go on a run and then things went downhill. She had to move into the clubhouse because her past came knocking and she needed help. Wrath wasn't sure what was going on but was pissed off about it and assumed the wrong thing and never would listen to her and they ended up no longer being together. They lived in the same clubhouse hating and secretly loving each other but neither willing to take the chance to mend the wrongs. Until one day Wrath decides he needs to be close to her again. He has his work cut out for him. This will not be a easy reconciliation that's for sure.<br /><br />Will Wrath get Trinity back? Will they be able to get over all the hurts from their past? Will they learn to trust each other? Will Trinity finally be able to explain to Wrath why she needed to move in there? <br /><br />This is a long and gripping book. You learn bits and pieces about Trinity and Wrath's lives throughout the book, its not just thrown out there. This book has a natural flow to it that makes it feel like it is happening in real life and not just a story you are reading. I could feel all the hurt as if it was happening to me. There were times that I just wanted to punch Wrath in the throat or balls because he pissed me off so bad but I loved him at the same time. If only he would've taken the time to listen. Then again I wanted to shake Trinity for not demanding he listen but as the story progressed I realize why she didn't. Anyways, I'm telling you this is a MUST read!!! Don't miss out on this book.<br /><br />I received and ARC in exchange for an honest review.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12253230127184119590" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1347614362" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1347614362" />
    <a title="Rachel" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31352280-rachel"><img alt="Rachel" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1425440929p2/31352280.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1347614362?book_show_action=true">Jul 28, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel" href="/user/show/31352280-rachel">Rachel</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780990794561" href="/book/show/23662114-tattered-on-my-sleeve">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1347614362" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14864278145116616313">Ahhh Wrath and Trinity's story is finally here! I've been waiting for this since the minute I finished the last book and these two did not disappoint! Wrath is every bit the hard ass biker with an attitude that we see in the previous books of this series. Trinity is still the girl behind the men...taking care of the club house and the guys themselves. She owns who she is and plays by the same rules as the guys, which was good to see in a female lead. I had several moments where I wanted to reach</span>
  <span id="freeText14864278145116616313" style="display:none">Ahhh Wrath and Trinity's story is finally here! I've been waiting for this since the minute I finished the last book and these two did not disappoint! Wrath is every bit the hard ass biker with an attitude that we see in the previous books of this series. Trinity is still the girl behind the men...taking care of the club house and the guys themselves. She owns who she is and plays by the same rules as the guys, which was good to see in a female lead. I had several moments where I wanted to reach through my kindle screen and slap the crap out of both Wrath and Trinity and lock them in a room together until they got their shit together. To say emotions ran high in this book would be an understatement. I was hurting right along side them while they tried to one up each other in the heart break department and smiling with them as they overcame roadblocks. Who knew Wrath could have a sweet side? Or that Trinity could be vulnerable while still standing on her own? I also enjoyed seeing more from the other guys and can't wait to see more from this series. Just like the other books in this series, Autumn left us with a "happy for now" ending...leaving the door open for adding more to their story. Have I mentioned I can't wait to read more Lost Kings?<br /><br />**An ARC as provided for my honest review**<br /><br />Rachel<br />Bestie Book Blog<br />bestiebookblog.com</span>
  <a data-text-id="14864278145116616313" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('87MmIdHm/pwdX8kxPqYbHWPZA3vYkpG9jie2yirFSN/s1DwBjCMf7wTUX0wjQi27W4eoqMraPRkWHm5/dP8QAw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('9Wt5u8aiPhCKFN8djBxyQMSd5eIfM+TDyTpgbWJWqWTqDGObm2ffY5OfSWCR+ETm/MNOMQ17SGdRA7jYPGzxuA==')})
  }

He signed up to be a prospect for the Lost Kings MC because it seemed like a fun way to get closer to her. Now that he’s gotten a taste of MC life, he’s not so sure this is where he belongs. With more than miles between them, will the deceptions they’ve lived with for so long be too much to overcome?
